The Case of Shi Jiurong: Interrogation of the Kidnappers; Shi Resigns and Goes to Beiping After the Incident; Zhang Sanjiuzi Suddenly Changes His Testimony

Shi Jiurong, a native of Ningbo and head of the sales department of the Meitong Motor Company at the intersection of Foch Road and Route Mercier, was kidnapped at 9:00 AM on April 18th of this year. He was traveling from his residence in his own car to the Meitong Motor Company for work. Upon arriving at the front of the building, four kidnappers suddenly rushed up to attempt to kidnap him. However, the attempt was unsuccessful because the Indian police officer manning the traffic light noticed the event, sounded an alarm, and the kidnappers got out of the car and fled in all directions, firing shots while resisting arrest, wounding the Indian police officer in the leg. As a result, one of the kidnappers, Tian Dazhong, was shot dead by patrol officers from the British and French concessions at the intersection of Route Ratard and Avenue Alber. After the incident, on the 24th of last month, Jin Jiulin, the chief inspector of the French Concession police, received a tip from an informant and arrested Zhang Sanjiuzi (39 years old, pulling rickshaws for a living and residing in a flat in Lujia, Nanshi), an accomplice of the kidnappers from Funing, on Route Lanwei. He was sent to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and detention for investigation. All details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the victim, Shi Jiurong, resigned from Meitong Company immediately after the incident and took his family to Beiping to make a living. The police investigation of Zhang's crime has been completed. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wang Gangxu of the Second Special District Court presided over the trial in the Second Criminal Court. Fei Xizhen, a lawyer from the Police Department, presented the case, prosecuting him for extortion under Article 347 of the Criminal Code. Subsequently, Zhou Buguang, an investigator, reported the arrest and investigation of the defendant. First, Li Alin (44 years old), Shi Jiurong's chauffeur from Yangzhou, testified that at the time, four kidnappers came, one holding a pistol, pointing it at my chest and telling me not to move, and one behind slapped me once not letting me raise my head. Later, because the car would not start, the police officer and a Russian mechanic in front of the door noticed, the kidnappers got out of the car and fled in all directions. At the time I was stunned and didn’t recognize the kidnappers. I do not recognize the defendant in this case. My right ear was deafened at the time and has not recovered. Next, Tian Zonglang, the informant, who is also the younger brother of the deceased kidnapper Tian Dazhong, testified, 24 years old, living at 219 Ankang Lane, Guangzhao Road, Zhabei, making a living pulling rickshaws. My brother Tian Dazhong was always in his hometown and came to Shanghai in January of this year. Later, Zhang Sanjiuzi often came to my house, sometimes several times a day, introducing my brother to an “old man” to recommend business. On the twelfth day of the third month of the lunar calendar, Zhang came to my house, had lunch, and at one o’clock, called my brother out together, and he never came home after that. Later, I heard people say that the appearance and clothing of the kidnapper who was shot dead was the same as my brother, but I did not dare to recognize him. I looked for Zhang for many days. One day I met Zhang in the rickshaw company on Hengfeng Road and asked him where my brother was. He said that he had already returned to Jiangbei, and he had sent him to the dock. I wrote a letter home to ask my mother, and recently a fellow villager came to Shanghai and said that my brother had not returned home. I looked for Zhang again but couldn't find him, so I went to my uncle Tian Yao to inquire. My uncle knows Zhang and knows where he is, so on September 22nd, he reported to the police station, took out more than a dozen photos of the deceased, and recognized the photo of my brother. Later, the detective arrested Zhang. Tian Yao's testimony was the same. When Zhang Sanjiuzi was interrogated, he flatly denied calling Tian Dazhong out and did not know about the kidnapping. He repeatedly cried injustice. He said that he had been pulling rickshaws in the Ma Sanhe rickshaw company at the eastern end of Xieqiao. On April 18th, he worked the early shift, going out at 6:00 AM and handing over the shift at 12:00 PM. The judge asked, "Were you sentenced to eight years in prison by the Provisional Court for a robbery case in 1927?" Zhang replied yes. At this point, Detective Zhou reported that the defendant had confessed at the police station that when the kidnapping took place, he was standing guard nearby, that a retired chauffeur from the Meitong Motor Company named Lao Qiang had drawn the line, and that the instigator was Li Zongqing, who lived in a flat in Qing'an Lane, Fangxie Road, and that the ringleader was Sun Xiaowuzi, who lived at 76 Route du Père Labour. When they went to arrest them at the addresses, they had already fled. The confession made by the defendant at the police station was recorded in a statement submitted to the court for inspection. The judge interrogated the defendant again, who still firmly denied confessing to participating in the kidnapping at the police station. The court reviewed the confession and ordered that the interrogation be adjourned to the 26th. The defendant was returned to custody.

Assassination of Tang Jiapeng: Examination of Gu Zhuxuan's Mental Illness; Investigation by the French Concession Police and Prosecution by the Court; Gu Flatly Denies at the First Trial

—The Court Appoints Famous Doctors to Examine Whether Gu Has Mental Illness—

Tang Jiapeng, formerly manager of the Great World entertainment complex and a native of Dinghai, nicknamed A Yu, was assassinated at 1:20 AM on June 18, 1933, when returning home from work at the Great World. As he walked out of the Great World with two or three friends to his car at the entrance, he was suddenly shot by several thugs, sustaining five bullet wounds and dying instantly at the age of 44. At the same time, a passerby, Wu Guangcai, was killed by a stray bullet. A month or so after the incident, the French Concession police successively arrested two criminals from Funing, Zhang Tinggui, also known as Xiao Sizi, and Zhao Guangfu from Yangzhou, and seized a pistol used by Zhao to kill Tang. As a result of the prosecution, Zhang was sentenced to 20 years in prison and Zhao to life imprisonment. After appeals, the sentences were finalized. During the execution of the sentences, Zhao reported to the French Concession Police Department that Wang Xinggao was the mastermind of the case. The police dispatched detectives to arrest Wang at the Central Hotel on December 13 of last year. After interrogation by the Second Special District Court, Wang was sentenced to life imprisonment. Wang refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the Third Branch of the High Court. After two court hearings, the evidence is currently under investigation. During this period, Zhao Guangfu submitted a petition to the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court, accusing Gu Zhuxuan, the owner of the Da Chan Stage and a native of Yancheng, of instigating murder, and requesting that he be summoned for interrogation. After receiving the petition, the court had Judge Zhang Chaozuo open a court session and bring the self-prosecutor Zhao to the case, informing him that the crime of murder did not comply with the self-prosecution procedure and should be reported to the Police Department for public prosecution. The self-prosecution was ruled inadmissible. Zhao immediately complied and reported to the French Concession Police Department. After the Police Department interrogated Zhao, it requested the Second Special District Court to issue an arrest warrant for Gu Zhuxuan. At noon on the 10th of last month, Chinese and Western detectives went to the First Special District Court with the arrest warrant to request police assistance. After registering, they went with detectives dispatched from the Central Police Station to Gu's residence at 9 Yonghe Lane, 222 North Xizang Road, arrested Gu, and brought him back to the French Concession Police Department. The next day, he was transferred to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and detention for investigation. On the 27th of the same month, Criminal Court President Wang Gangxu, together with Prosecutor Wang Ren and Clerk Zheng Rong, specially opened the First Criminal Court for trial. The lawyer from the French Concession Police Department prosecuted Gu for instigating murder in accordance with Articles 29 and 271 of the Criminal Code. Tang Youmei, the younger sister of the deceased Tang Jiapeng, also hired a lawyer to file an incidental private lawsuit, seeking damages. When Gu Zhuxuan was interrogated, he flatly denied instigating murder and claimed that he did not know the accuser Zhao Guangfu or Zhang Tinggui. The court then ordered that Zhao Guangfu, Zhang Tinggui, and Wang Xinggao, as well as Xue Zhenyi, who was related to the case (attempted to kill Hai Zongqi, the head of the First Rescue Team of the Red Cross, in April 1932, and was sentenced to seven years in prison and is currently serving his sentence), be brought to the case and interrogated one by one. The court adjourned the hearing, stating that it still needed to investigate the evidence in the case. The defense lawyers for the defendant Gu Zhuxuan, Xue Dubi, Wu Kaisheng, and Lin Dawen, stated that the defendant suffered from psychosis while in custody, making it inconvenient to delay medical treatment, and requested permission to grant bail for him to seek medical treatment outside. The court said it would wait for a decision. It is now known that the court attaches great importance to this case and has specially invited a German doctor, a well-known psychiatrist in Shanghai, and the court's medical officer to go to the Guangci Hospital a few days ago to conduct a detailed examination of Gu Zhuxuan, which lasted a long time before returning. It is said that the court will wait for the expert opinion of the medical officer and others to be submitted to the court for review before it can set a date for the retrial.

Another Creditor Sues Ou Jiancheng Et Al.; Lin Kanghou Granted Dismissal; Part of Ou Jiancheng's Case Rejected

—The Presiding Judge Also Announces the Reasons for the Judgment—

Ou Jiancheng, the general manager of the Yong'an Silver Company, which has already gone bankrupt, and Lin Kanghou, a director of the company, were sued by creditors for embezzlement and fraud. The First Special District Court sentenced Ou to one year in prison and Lin to a fine. The trial of the other directors of the company who could not be summoned was suspended. Now, two more creditors, Liu Keshan and Shi Chengde, jointly sued Ou Jiancheng, Lin Kanghou, and Zhang Zilian for fraud. The First Special District Court opened a court session yesterday afternoon with Judge Xiao presiding. Only Lin Kanghou and his defense lawyer appeared in court. Ou and Zhang, the two defendants, failed to appear despite being summoned. After the plaintiffs stated the process of the deposit being embezzled, Lin's lawyer immediately defended, stating that Lin was neither a shareholder nor a manager of the company, but only a nominal director, and should not be held responsible. He requested that Lin be found not guilty. Lin also stated that he was also one of the victims. He felt very aggrieved by the fine imposed on him last time. He had never received a criminal penalty. As for whether he should be liable for repaying the debt, it should be determined after the Civil Court determines his status as a director. After questioning, Judge Xiao immediately announced that Lin Kanghou would be dismissed. The plaintiff's incidental civil lawsuit against Lin Kanghou was rejected, and part of Ou Jiancheng's case was not accepted. The trial of Zhang Zilian's case was suspended. Judge Xiao also announced the reasons for the judgment in court, stating that although the civil lawsuit against Lin was rejected today, it did not prevent the plaintiff from filing an independent civil lawsuit in the Civil Court. Ou Jiancheng had previously been sentenced to imprisonment, and the facts of the crime now sued were completely the same as the previous case, so it would not be accepted again. As for Zhang Zilian's address being unknown and never appearing in court, the trial had been suspended previously, so the case would remain the same.

Japanese Dance Hall: Italian Sailors Resort to Violence; Flee Without Paying for Dance Tickets; Two Japanese People Beaten

According to the Japanese newspaper "Japanese Daily News," at 9:30 PM on the 7th, three Italian sailors entered the Lion Dance Hall on Zhaipu Road. They first drank a bottle of beer and then danced with the dance hostesses. After about an hour, they wanted to leave. The dance hostess said that the tickets paid were not enough for three, and asked them to pay the difference. The sailors did not care. When they were walking to the stairs, they suddenly bumped into two Japanese expatriates, Fukami and Oda. The sailors immediately beat Fukami violently. Oda saw this and stepped forward to stop them, but was also affected. The sailors saw that blood was flowing from the mouths and noses of the two and knew that they had caused trouble. They quickly took rickshaws and fled south. By the time the police from the Japanese Consulate General arrived after hearing the news, the sailors were gone. They took the victims to Fumin Hospital for treatment.

Yiyixuan, a Historical Institution, Raided for Gambling and Smoking; More Than a Dozen Men and Women Together Gambling; Two or Three Addicts Enjoying the Pleasures of Opium

—Smokers All Detained and Sent to Court—

The Yiyixuan General Association at 5 Sanhe Lane, 412 Jiangxi Road, was founded during the reign of Emperor Xuantong at the end of the Qing Dynasty, nearly 30 years ago. The members of the club are mostly wealthy Cantonese merchants in Shanghai, and political figures occasionally visit when they are in the mood. Because the club holds a special permit, the police authorities consider it a high-class entertainment venue, so they rarely inspect it. However, recently it has turned into a den of gambling and smoking, with people gambling and smoking day and night. Anyone who is not a member of the association can enter to gamble and smoke. Xu Shuyong, a head constable from the responsible police station, and Jiang Shangpei, a detective, secretly investigated and confirmed this, and requested the First Special District Court to issue a search warrant. They rushed to search the premises at 6:30 PM on the 7th. More than a dozen men and two fashionable women were gambling intensely. The famous Southern singer Jiu Xuebing was also among the gamblers. In addition, there were opium addicts Wang Shaoli, Hu Tian, Zhang Guo, Tan Gui from Yangzhou, all lying on beds, enjoying the pleasures of opium. The head constable and others immediately took the four smokers, along with six opium pipes, four opium lamps, 145 and a half taels of opium paste, and two jars of opium ash, back to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special District Court, where Judge Qian interrogated them. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the police station, stated that Wang and Tan were accused of violating Article 6 of the Anti-Opium Law, and Hu and Zhang were accused of violating Article 11 of the Anti-Opium Law. He requested an investigation. The defendants Wang Shaoli and Tan Gui one said he worked as a bookkeeper at the club, and the other said he was a tea server at the club. All the opium paste was brought by the members themselves to smoke at the club. Hu Tian flatly denied having an opium addiction, and Zhang Guo admitted without hesitation to smoking opium. After reviewing the confessions, the court ordered that the two defendants Wang and Tan be detained pending further investigation. Hu Tian was found not guilty, and Zhang Guo was fined 60 yuan, which could be commuted to one day of labor service for every two yuan. Before the execution, he was sent to an opium addiction treatment hospital for 20 days of abstinence. The opium paraphernalia was confiscated.

The Meifeng Liquidation Office: Refunds Small Deposits; Checks Have All Been Sent Out

According to the Shanghai Times, the Meifeng Bank Liquidation Office moved from its original address at 29 Nanjing Road to the Dalai Building on Guangdong Road on Sunday. The bank's deposits of less than 50 yuan were previously decided to be repaid in full. Now the checks have all been sent out, so the procedure is nearing completion. According to liquidator He Fu, the liquidation of the bank will take about two years to complete, because many huge assets cannot be easily converted into cash, and debts owed to the bank cannot be easily collected. If it is rushed, the interests of the depositors will be sacrificed.

Opium Offenders in Concessions: All Sent to Municipal Hospital for Abstinence; After 20 Days of Abstinence, Sent Back to Court for Execution

The city's anti-opium campaign has been organized by the Municipal Government's Anti-Opium Committee, which has selected prominent Shanghai figures as members to plan and implement the campaign. The Municipal Public Security Bureau is registering opium addicts. The government and the people are cooperating to eliminate opium addiction within the specified time. However, the first step of the work can only be implemented in the Chinese area. Opium addicts within the concessions cannot be ordered to register according to regulations. These people compare themselves to those living outside the law, with opium addiction a deeply rooted habit, stubbornly refusing to change. This has led those originally living in the Chinese area to think that the "Peach Blossom Spring" is nearby and to move to the concessions. If each goes its own way, the prohibition will be lax and the differences will be significant. Even if opium addiction is eliminated in the Chinese area in the future, the number of opium addicts in the concessions will increase, hindering the progress of the anti-opium campaign and violating the original intention of eradicating opium completely. Mayor Wu Tiecheng had already seen this problem, so he repeatedly discussed cooperation with the authorities of the Public Concession to implement a solution. Fortunately, the foreigners also recognized that the opium disaster urgently needed to be eradicated and agreed to work together to help us complete the anti-opium plan. After obtaining the understanding of the concession authorities, Mayor Wu immediately sent a letter to the First Special District Court, notifying it that after adjudicating opium cases in the future, the opium offenders in the case should first be ordered by the police to be sent to the opium addiction treatment hospital run by the Municipal Government for 20 days of abstinence. After the term expires, they should be sent back to the court for execution of the imposed penalty. This measure has been implemented since yesterday. Opium addicts in the concessions may be able to avoid registration, but if they are detained, in addition to being punished, they will also be subject to abstinence treatment. It is hoped that opium addicts will voluntarily quit, because today, talismans are really not to be relied on.

Health Bureau Requests Appropriation: Rebuild the Municipal Shanghai Hospital; Design Similar to the Municipal Central Hospital; Equipment Also Expanded; Budget Requires 100,000 Yuan

The Municipal Health Bureau, due to the dilapidated buildings and simple equipment of the Municipal Shanghai Hospital on Duojia Road in Nanshi, has specially requested the Municipal Government to allocate about 100,000 yuan for the demolition and reconstruction of the hospital and the expansion of equipment. It is heard that the design of the hospital is similar to that of the Municipal Central Hospital, so not only will the construction project be large, but the equipment will also be more complete than other hospitals in the city. It is expected that after the completion of the hospital, the patients in Nanshi will feel much more convenient.

French Concession: Tram Lines 17 and 18 Return to Original Route

The roads on Route Lafayette and Route de Marche (near Taiping Bridge) in the French Concession have been rebuilt and raised by the Public Works Department of the French Municipal Council. Tram lines 17 and 18 of the French Tram Company have temporarily changed their routes, turning from Route Lanwei to Zhao Zhou Road, which connects the Chinese area and the French Concession, and going north directly to the Great World. Southbound vehicles still travel on the original route. Now that the roads have been completely completed, tram lines 17 and 18 have returned to their original routes yesterday, turning from Route de Marche to Rue de l'Avenir, going out of Nanyang Bridge to the north, directly to the Great World, and entering the Public Concession.

North German Company Transfers the "Stuttgart" from the Atlantic to Replace Service to the Far East; Construction of Third New Ship Delayed; Postponed for One Month Before Launching

The North German Company is building three new high-speed 18,000-ton ships to increase the frequency of express mail ships to the Far East. The two ships that have been completed and launched are the "Scharnhorst" and "Potsdam." The name of the third ship has been decided to be "Gneisenau," which is the same style as the previous two ships and is a sister ship on the Europe-Asia line. The third ship "Gneisenau," which runs the Far East Express between Germany and China, was originally scheduled to officially join the Europe-Asia line on December 4th. Because of the launch of the three new ships, the North German Company will suspend five passenger ships originally traveling to the Far East, namely the "Saar," "Derfflinger," "Fulda," and "Trier." However, the third ship, the "Gneisenau," cannot be launched on December 4th due to construction in the dock. But the schedule has been arranged, and a mail ship must come to Shanghai this month. Now the local branch of Melchers & Co. has received a telegram from the North German Company in Bremen, Germany, that the new ship "Gneisenau" must be postponed for one month before it can be completed and launched. The special express mail ship scheduled for December 4th has now been decided by the company to have the "Stuttgart," a first-class mail ship sailing on the Atlantic Ocean, replace it. The ship has a net tonnage of 13,397 tons (ship shown in another picture), and the passenger accommodations inside are also very beautiful, similar to the three new ships, but the speed is 18 nautical miles per hour, which is slightly slower than the express ships. It is scheduled to depart on December 4th and come to Shanghai, without stopping at Rangoon or Penang along the way. After arriving in Shanghai, it will not go to Japan, but will stay in Shanghai for three days and then return to Europe. As for the new ship "Gneisenau," it has been rescheduled to come to the Far East on New Year's Day next year.

Reporter Li Chuanbin of the Central News Agency Killed in a Tragic Accident: Westerner's Car Crashes onto Sidewalk; Shop Windows Also Destroyed

The Central News Agency reports that Li Chuanbin (Zi: Renlin), a radio operator at the Shanghai branch of the Central News Agency, was traveling from his dormitory in Tongan Lane, Hankou Road, to the branch office in the Continental Commercial Center at 2:10 PM yesterday when a car driven by a foreigner (Concession Permit No. 8497) traveling from west to east suddenly crashed onto the sidewalk in front of the Fuhe Yong Flag & Banner Shop at 421 Hankou Road (next to the Shanghai Hotel), destroying the glass doors and windows of the shop. Li was walking on the sidewalk at the time and was knocked down from behind by the car, suffering severe injuries to his legs and internal organs. He only cried for help once before losing consciousness. The Fuhe Yong Shop quickly called the police and the Red Cross to send an ambulance. Emergency treatment was immediately administered, and he was taken to Renji Hospital on Shandong Road, but he died of his injuries at the hospital at about 5:00 PM. Li was from Wuxian, Jiangsu, and was only 23 years old. He graduated from the Shanghai Radio Training School and was a radio operator at the Lanzhou Station of the Eurasia Aviation Company. Even more tragic, Li had just gotten engaged the day before. His brother, Yunlin, who works at the Suzhou Telephone Bureau, has been notified by the Central News Agency by telegram and will come to Shanghai this morning to take care of the funeral arrangements.

"Haimen" Ship Converted into Patrol Ship: Purchased by Zhejiang Fisheries Police Bureau for 12,000 Yuan and Immediately Docked for Major Repairs

The "Haimen" ship was originally owned by the former Jufeng Shipping Company and sailed the Shanghai-Chongming route. It joined the Shensha United Bureau and was later purchased by the Wuhe Shipping Company, which was jointly formed by five companies including Huqi Line Da and Ping'an. It was docked in the Huangpu River. It has now been sold to the Zhejiang Fisheries Police Bureau for 12,000 yuan. Because it has been out of service for three years, it has been decided to dock it for major repairs and convert it into a patrol ship.

City Government: Strictly Prohibits Civil Servants from Riding for Free

The Municipal Government, in order to strictly prohibit civil servants from riding vehicles for free, issued a special order to all its affiliated agencies yesterday, regarding a case reported by the Public Utilities Bureau stating that the Beijing-Shanghai-Suzhou Private Long-Distance Bus Company Joint Association reported, "Upon investigation, member long-distance bus companies have preferential treatment for military and police personnel riding their buses. As for local party and government agencies, it is also common to provide complimentary tickets, which has been a long-standing practice. Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Government investigated the aforementioned situation and issued a public notice prohibiting the practice, except for military and police personnel who are allowed to purchase half-price tickets. The Municipal Government has always strictly prohibited free rides. Now that the Provincial Government has explicitly banned it and the provincial and municipal routes are connected, for the sake of convenient implementation, we have copied the original text of the Provincial Government's public notice and submitted it to your bureau, requesting you to forward it to the Municipal Government to reiterate the previous order so that all companies can comply, which would be in the public interest." Attached is the public notice of the Jiangsu Provincial Government and a notice from the Highway Administration Office of the Department of Construction, stating that commercial long-distance bus companies often issue free tickets indiscriminately to curry favor with local party, government, military, and police personnel. This kind of behavior not only hinders the company's operations but also relates to the discipline of civil servants, which is quite inappropriate. Now that the Jiangsu Provincial Government has issued a strict prohibition, our city should follow suit. It is proposed that your director, in conjunction with the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, issue a public notice to prohibit this practice in order to maintain business and rectify discipline. Is this appropriate? We have copied the public notice of the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the notice from the Highway Administration Office of the province and submitted them for your review and implementation." Upon review, the matter concerns the maintenance of transportation, and it should be approved. In addition to sending a letter to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters to jointly issue a public notice and separate orders, this order is hereby issued for your compliance. This order."

Owner of Xianda Silk Store, Zhou Qixin, Sued for Issuing Bad Checks; Defendant Absent Without Reason, Rescheduled for Retrial

The Guowen News Agency reports that Xianda Silk Store, located at No. 9, Lane 6, Huashunli, Tongfu Road, is a sole proprietorship owned by Zhou Qixin from Wuxian County. In June of this year, Zhou issued a check for 413 yuan payable on July 10, drawn on his account at the Jing'an Temple Road branch of the Shanghai Bank, to Renji Silk Store, located in Longxingli, Xiangfen Lane, North Zhejiang Road, which is now closed and being liquidated, to repay part of the debt for goods. Upon presentation, the bank refused to pay due to insufficient funds. Ni Lanping, the manager of Renji Silk Store, repeatedly negotiated with the issuer, Zhou Qixin. Zhou attempted to offset the check amount with debts owed to him by Mao Pengnian, an employee of Renji Silk Store. Ni argued that according to commercial custom, private dealings were irrelevant to the business, and according to Article 10 of the Negotiable Instruments Law, the obligor of a negotiable instrument may not assert against the holder any defense based on his own dealings with the drawer or a prior holder. Ni believed that Zhou Qixin issued a check that was not honored upon maturity and attempted to offset it with private debts, which was clearly improper. Therefore, he retained lawyer Zhang Shijie to file a criminal self-accusation with the Shanghai First Special District Local Court, requesting that Zhou be punished for issuing bad checks, and also filed an incidental civil suit. At 2:00 PM yesterday, Judge Huang Daxi heard the case in Criminal Court No. 5. Lawyer Zhang Shijie and the accuser, Ni Lanping, arrived on time, but the defendant, Zhou Qixin, did not appear, nor was he represented by a defense attorney. After Judge Huang questioned the accuser, lawyer Zhang stated the intention of the prosecution and requested that the defendant be strictly summoned to court, as the defendant had been legally summoned by the court but failed to appear without a valid reason. The court ordered that the case be rescheduled for retrial at 3:00 PM on October 26, pending the defendant's appearance. The court was then adjourned.

Weather Report

Xujiahui Observatory: Yesterday's weather forecast at 4:30 PM stated that the sky around Shandong was cloudy and sunny, with varying southwest to northwest winds. The weather in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River was cloudy and overcast, with occasional rain, with strong southeast to northeast light winds. The weather in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River gradually cleared, with gentle northeast to northwest winds. The sky in the East China Sea and Taiwan was overcast, with showers and strong northeast winds. The center of the hurricane at 1:00 PM yesterday had reached within about 60 miles of 22 degrees north latitude and 109 degrees east longitude, moving northwest-west. The wind force is unknown. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 80.2 and the lowest was 60.8. On the same day last year, the highest was 79.0 and the lowest was 51.8.

Special Item

Shanghai's First Literacy School Operations (5)

— Wu Tiecheng

5. Prospects for the Second Session of Literacy Education

Promoting [literacy] is an innovation in most provinces and cities. This city has a responsibility to do its best. The large-scale nature of this undertaking means that the government cannot bear all the material and human resources alone. Borrowing and utilizing school buildings and equipment are unavoidable in practice. Those who cling to old habits and make excuses to shirk responsibility are expected to discard their personal prejudices and fully support this undertaking. We hope that everyone in the society will work together to promote this undertaking. This is the first hope for people in the society. The Literacy Education Committee has set up offices in various districts, with various committees such as investigation, publicity, and academic affairs. The goal is to gather the wisdom of the Party, government, police, and schools and turn them into a strong force. However, in the beginning, they are able to engage in the work earnestly, but over time, they may become complacent. As the saying goes, "Make the beginning, make the end." We still hope that they will maintain their initial enthusiasm and be truly responsible. This is the second hope for the responsible people in each district. The quality of teachers greatly affects the students' interest in learning and their learning efficiency. Most of the teachers in this city's literacy schools have been selected and trained and should be able to fulfill their duties happily. However, according to reports, there are also a few who are perfunctory, do not seek improvement, or have improper teaching behavior, or even use force or rely on police force. It is important for teachers to guide and influence students with their personality. They should improve their moral character and seek improvement in teaching in order to set a good example. They must not be casual or perfunctory, resulting in shoddy work. In addition to establishing reward and punishment measures and strict assessment, we still hope that all members will strive to improve themselves. This is the third hope for teachers. As mentioned earlier, past inspections have been conducted. In the future, in addition to continuing to conduct inspections as before, full-time inspectors will be assigned to supervise the process. Special attention should be paid to the review of results, both during the normal course and at the end of the term. However, education should progress step by step and emphasize consistency to achieve consistent results. This is the fourth hope for inspectors at all levels to work hard. According to the situation of the first literacy schools, there are quite a few private schools. If they can seriously handle all aspects of teaching and supervision and continue to run them, so that quality and quantity have the same progress, then the power of society to assist the government in promoting this undertaking will also be considerable. As for the service team approach, it is not without feasibility in principle, but the reason why the effectiveness is not obvious is that the methods still need to be carefully considered. We should continue to consult and seek improvement. This is the fifth hope for those who are enthusiastic about literacy schools to continue to move forward. The number of graduates from the first municipal private literacy schools will be more than 60,000. In order to continue to advance the studies of those who are ambitious and the general qualified students, starting from the second session, each school will add a class of advanced literacy classes, and plans to run popular literacy reading materials, so that they can review the old and learn the new, and achieve lasting results. This is also the sixth aspect of this city's promotion of literacy education, which emphasizes the consistent and complementary approach. Starting from the second session, the teaching time will be extended to three months, and the substitute cadre system will be abolished, giving teachers a day off every two weeks, so as to take into account the facts, so that teachers can rest and students can learn fully, so as to improve teaching and gradually improve the results. To teach hard and learn hard, the achievement should be practical. This is the seventh hope for teachers and students to strive even harder. (End)

Letters to the Editor

Sir: I read in the news column of your newspaper an article about a Japanese man beating a rickshaw puller to death, stating that the rickshaw puller, Wang Deyuan, was from Taizhou, and that his family had reported to the fellow-countrymen association for assistance. Wang Deyuan is from our county, and his sister, Chen Wangshi, asked the association for assistance. The association convened a temporary meeting to decide on measures: (1) send a letter to the Japanese Consul General to punish the murderer, (2) provide compensation, (3) ensure that similar incidents do not happen again, (4) in addition to the public prosecution part, which will be filed by the police station, the association will also appoint lawyer Song Shixiang to represent the victim's family and pursue compensation for damages in accordance with the law. Because your newspaper misstated the victim's hometown, we are sending this letter to correct the record and clarify the truth. Sincerely, Taixian Fellow-Countrymen Association in Shanghai, Chairman Song Shixiang, October 8, 1935.

Thirty-Two Units Report In, National Games to Open Tomorrow Morning. Yesterday, Qinghai, Xikang, Xinjiang, Mongolia, Liaoning, Hebei, Zhejiang, and Nanjing Arrived. Six More Units Expected to Arrive Today.

The Sixth National Games are scheduled to open tomorrow morning. Representatives from various provinces and cities have been arriving and reporting. Yesterday, units including Qinghai, Xikang, Xinjiang, Mongolia, Liaoning, Hebei, Zhejiang, and Nanjing arrived. Currently, thirty-two units have reported to the organizing committee. Liaoning Athletes Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Liaoning athletes participating in the National Games are highly anticipated. It is reported that Liu Changchun and his party of five arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday afternoon at 3:30 PM. They have moved into the Games' accommodations. After all members arrive today, they will report to the organizing committee. Liu Xiaobie's arrival in Shanghai has not changed his demeanor. Many sports fans came to the venue to inquire about him.

Hebei's Heroes Have Balanced Strength

The Hebei Province delegation participating in the National Games consists of 120 athletes and staff, led by General Leader Zhao Wenzao. They departed from Tianjin at the end of last month and arrived in Pukou the night before last. They then transferred to the Shanghai-Nanjing express train and arrived in Shanghai at 11:00 AM yesterday morning, immediately reporting to the organizing committee.

General Leader Speaks: According to General Leader Zhao, speaking to reporters, since the Far Eastern Games in the 18th year of the Republic (1929), the public has paid great attention to sports. In recent years, the provincial government has vigorously promoted it, resulting in excellent results. To popularize sports in rural areas, the Hebei Provincial Regional Games were established. The province is divided into five regions, each with a director, designed by the Provincial Department of Education. The aim is to extend from urban higher schools to rural primary and secondary schools, and from rural primary and secondary schools to every citizen. This plan has already been implemented. It is expected that upon returning from these Games, the people of Hebei will have a deeper understanding of sports.

Xikang's Track and Field Results Are Remarkable

The Xikang team, which has never participated in the National Games, recently trained thirteen athletes two months ago to encourage the people there to be interested in sports and participated in this conference, led by General Leader Ma Zezhao. They arrived in Shanghai at 2:30 PM yesterday and immediately reported to the organizing committee.

Ma Zezhao Speaks: According to Ma, speaking to reporters, Xikang is located in a remote area, and the people there hardly know what sports are, especially modern sports. Other old-fashioned sports, such as horse riding and shooting, are still relatively common. As for swimming skills, they are almost the best in the country. The best can stay in the water for several days without any change, but unfortunately, the posture is not suitable and cannot be reported to the conference. There is also a skill of throwing stones. Usually, everyone can throw 60 meters away, and they can hit the target 100% of the time within 60 meters. The funds for participating in this conference were all raised from donations from various places. The purpose is not to win medals, but purely to see the skills of all-around athletes, so that the local sports can be improved upon returning to Xikang.

A Glimpse of Strength: The team fully participates in track and field. The list is as follows: General Leader Ma Zezhao, Instructor Zhao Guji, Administrator Sun Qinghua, Track and Field Athletes Mu Chenghua, Ma Shujun, Jia Maosen, Gao Guogui, Li Wenbi, Yang Changbo, Wang Xinlong, Wang Fude, He Qichang, Guo Zheng, Jia Maosen, 100 meters in 10.8 seconds, Mu Chenghua, 200 meters in 22.4 seconds, Wang Xinlong, 400 meters in 52.4 seconds, Wang Fude, 1500 meters in 5 minutes and 26 seconds. The results are quite remarkable.

Western sports are still in the early stages of learning. Most of the athletes participating this time are students from Mongolian and Tibetan schools and military schools. They are still interested in basketball, but they have no confidence in track and field. This time, they are just observing others. Except for the eight wrestlers who are still on the way, the rest of the team has arrived. Xinjiang Representatives Arrived Yesterday from Beijing

The Xinjiang delegation, consisting of twelve members, led by team leader Gong Bicheng, took the train from Beijing at 8 AM yesterday to Shanghai. The delegation includes General Leader Gong Bicheng, Instructor Zhang Qing, Administrator Sheng Yan, and athletes Mu Weixin, Ha Weixin, Su Jingxin, Ni Zuxin, Hai Huanxin, Wu Fanxin, Ou Nianxin, Pei Ziliang, Li Guanying, Han Zhenhua, and An Chongwen, participating in track and field and swimming. As for various techniques for riding through high mountains and wilderness, they are particularly skilled. Track and field and other sports have only been promoted in recent years. This is the second time Xinjiang has participated (the first time was in 1933). On the one hand, it is to see the excellent athletes from all over the country for reference, and on the other hand, it is to let people across the country know that Xinjiang people are the same as other provinces and cities and can participate in various events. Although they do not hope to win any medals, they want to show the people of Xinjiang's interest in sports and the spirit of bravely attending the meeting. In addition, some of the province's athletes arrived in Beijing half a year ago, and some are students studying in Beijing, so they all came from Beijing yesterday.

Considerable Strength, Few Highlights: Malayan Chinese Soccer Team Wins Against Youth Team with a Score of 3-0. The Youth Team Lost 2 Goals in the First Half. The Malayan Chinese Team Has Average Talent, but the Coordination Does Not Seem to Be Perfect.

The Malayan Chinese soccer team, attending the National Games, played a friendly match against the Youth soccer team yesterday at Shen Garden. However, the weather was uncooperative yesterday, with drizzle falling continuously. As it had not stopped by 3:00 PM, the National Sports Advancement Association believed that the competition would be difficult to complete due to the rain. Approximately four to five hundred soccer fans were let in. At 3:10 PM, the Malayan Chinese team finally arrived slowly, and ticket sales then began. Those who arrived early took great advantage of the situation. After defeating the Shanghai representative team, the Youth team was ambitious. Although they lost to the Malayan Chinese team yesterday, it was not their fault, but rather that their strength was slightly inferior. The score was 2-0 in the first half and 1-0 in the second half. The details of the battle are recorded as follows:

Opening Record

After the Malayan Chinese team kicked off in the center, they surged into the Youth defense like a landslide. The Youth team was not weak, and they desperately resisted the enemy. They managed to barely survive several dangerous moments. However, the Malayan Chinese team continued their efforts, and Yao Shenghua scored a goal, opening the record. The Youth team then tried to counterattack, but to no avail. Shi Cheng intercepted the ball in the middle and passed it to Xu Buyun, but he failed to break through the defenses.

Youth Pleases the Crowd

The Malayan Chinese team was not polite and bravely advanced. Guan Xinde took a long shot, and Xin Ziliang satisfied with his head to save it, but unexpectedly, the top of the head was dull, reflecting it into the goal. Gu Biao inexplicably lost his territory and let it into the net. Hu Yizhong was assisted by Jiang Zhaoxiang and attacked forward, but was saved by Zhen Lin.

Flowering on the Top

The battle resumed, Zhao Aisheng kissed the ball with his hand, and the referee enforced the law like a mountain. Xie Qingfu took a high shot and kicked it away, but Gu Biao caught it. Luo Douwen received a pass from Liu Zukan and shot it high outside the goal. Hu Yizhong had an excellent opportunity, but his header was too high. Zhao Aisheng showed his skills and saved Adou. Du Yadi passed to Xie Qingfu, flowering on the top, creating a total result of 3-0, the road of the Malayan Chinese team.

Observing Strength

The Malayan Chinese team did not field their official lineup yesterday, but their strength was still considerable. The talent is very average, but the coordination is not yet pure, and the footwork is also unfamiliar. Several times they could have won but did not. Judging from yesterday's actions, they were not as good as Hong Kong. Perhaps the first battle will not be very exciting. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

Tennis Exhibition Match Today: Lin Wangsu vs. Carson

Starting at 3:00 PM at Kangti Road. Also featuring a mixed doubles exhibition match between Wang Qiu vs. Yang Ruan.

The Shanghai Tennis Club, in order to increase interest in tennis, held an open tennis tournament. Malayan tennis master Lin Wangsu, due to the fatigue of the journey, lost to Xu Weipei. The club has scheduled Lin Wangsu to perform a singles match again this afternoon at the club's venue on Kangti Road. His opponent is Carson, the city's singles tennis champion. It is expected that there will be a fierce battle. In addition, there will be a mixed doubles exhibition match between Wang Wenzheng and Qiu Feihai against Yang Lunzhang and Ruan Guoying. Tickets are divided into two types, one yuan and half yuan. The competition starts at 3:00 PM. The program is recorded as follows:

Mixed Doubles Exhibition (Starting at 3:00 PM)

Wang Wenzheng vs. Yang Lunzhang

Qiu Feihai vs. Ruan Guoying

Singles Exhibition

Lin Wangsu vs. Carlsson

Guangdong Soccer Team vs. British Allied Forces at Shen Garden at 3:00 PM This Afternoon

The Guangdong soccer team, due to the absence of four knights, Huang Jiliang, Li Tiansheng, Ye Beihua, and Hong Jingxiang, has suffered a great impact on its strength, especially in previous recordings. In order to practice, the team has scheduled to play against the British Army Joint (Innis West Mixed Team) at Shen Garden at 3:00 PM this afternoon. The Guangdong team's lineup is as follows:

12th Army Polo Team Has Set Off

(Baoding, 8th dispatch) The 12th Army polo team, consisting of eight members and seventeen horses, departed on the 7th to Shanghai to participate in the National Games.

Arrangements for Children Performing Tai Chi Exercises to Take the Train

The following are the regulations for the 6th National Games for transporting children performing Tai Chi exercises by train:

(1) All team leaders and children participating in the Tai Chi performance will travel by train, with two separate transportations.

(A) Arrival: The first train will depart from the South Station at 6:30 AM and from Xujiahui at 6:40 AM, going directly to the Sanmin Road station at the venue (arriving at 8:00 AM). The second train will depart from the North Station at 8:05 AM, from Tiantong'an Station at 8:11 AM, and from Jiangwan Station at 8:19 AM, going directly to the Sanmin Road station at the venue (arriving at 8:32 AM). (B) Return to Shanghai: The first train will depart from the Sanmin Road station at 4:35 PM, arriving at Xujiahui at 6:00 PM and at the South Station at 6:10 PM. The second train will depart from the Sanmin Road station at 3:50 PM, arriving at Jiangwan at 4:05 PM, at Tiantong'an at 4:17 PM, and at the North Station at 4:25 PM. (2) At each station, personnel from the China Travel Service will work with the stationmaster to check the number of students from each school boarding the train.

(3) Each school must adhere to the train schedules for each station. The train will not wait for latecomers.

(4) Form a column when entering the station and boarding the train to facilitate counting.

(5) Team leaders and children must wear Tai Chi uniforms. The first train departing from the South Station will carry a total of 1,600 people from (19 schools):

Wanzhu, Yangzheng, Shangwen, Xicheng, Wuben, Shihua, Bide, Jingye, Tonghui, Nongtan, Nanjin, Dongming, Minglun, Jiangjing, Meixi, Chongzheng, Cangji, Xunyu, and Deyuan. A total of 50 people from (1 school) will board at Xujiahui:

Honglu. The second train departing from the North Station will carry a total of 700 people from (8 schools): He'an, Minzhi, Tongshan, Shanghai Elementary School, Shuji, Yude, Feihong, and Peiben. A total of 550 people from (6 schools) will board from Tiantong'an Station: Yucai, Qimei, Haishan, Chengzhong, Ningbo, and First Elementary School. A total of 100 people from (2 schools) will board from Jiangwan Station: Qiujiang and Zhongshan. The above 36 schools total 3,000 people.

Notes: (1) The organizing committee will not send separate notices to each school regarding transportation arrangements. (2) In addition to the team leader, each school may send one guardian per small team. (3) After the performance, the prize distribution group will distribute airplane-shaped "Good Student" pencils manufactured by the China Pencil Factory, one pencil to each participating child and one box to each participating school, as a souvenir. (4) Each school must provide its own refreshments.

Guests for National Games Opening Ceremony Must Wear Formal Attire

The opening ceremony of the Sixth National Games will be held at 10:00 AM on October 10th at the Shanghai Central Sports Field. As the National Games is a state event, Chairman Lin, President Wang, and the ministers of the central government, as well as ambassadors and ministers from various countries, will attend. The ceremony will be exceptionally grand. According to the person in charge of the National Games Preparatory Committee, all Chinese and foreign guests who have received invitations, except for ordinary spectators, must wear uniforms with medals, morning coats, or blue gowns with black mandarin jackets to show respect for the occasion.

Yesterday's Reception for Malayan Chinese Athletes included a Visit to the Sites of the Songhu Battle

Mayor Wu Welcomes Guests at a Tea Party at City Hall

The Shanghai Education Bureau, the Social Affairs Bureau, the China Aviation Association, and 97 other organizations, forming the Preparatory Committee for Welcoming Overseas Chinese Athletes from Malaya, hired 50 Xiang Sheng automobiles yesterday at 1:00 PM to host all the athletes for a tour of the city. The details are as follows:

Departure: At 1:30 PM, all the cars gathered in front of the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School on Xiangyin Road. Beforehand, each car had been assigned a number, and a small yellow welcoming flag was inserted in front of each car. At 1:00 PM sharp, the departure began, led by the Eight Trigram car of Tiger Balm Wing On Tong, followed closely by the private cars of Hu Wenhu, Hu Guigeng, Lu Lihua, and others. Next came the cars carrying the athletes, totaling about 60 vehicles, proceeding in single file, resembling a long snake formation, quite a sight to behold. Citizens on the road stood and watched. After reaching the YMCA at Eight Immortals Bridge, the reception desk provided a tour route map to each person (with Mayor Wu's inscription on the cover).

Tour Route: After the official departure, the motorcade headed south to the West Gate, passed by the Chen Ying Shi Memorial Tower, and proceeded along Zhonghua Road to the Wenwen Park. Unexpectedly, the weather turned unfavorable, and heavy rain started to fall, making it inconvenient to get off the cars for a visit. So, the motorcade went from the Wenmiao Park, along Zhonghua Road, directly to Gaochang Temple to visit the Jiangnan Shipyard and the Naval Aircraft Factory. The factory director warmly received the guests and personally led them to visit various departments. Leaving the Jiangnan Shipyard, the motorcade turned onto Zhizaoju Road, passed through Jinzhou Road and Minguo Road, entered Zhejiang Road, turned east onto Nanjing Road to the Bund, turned north onto the Bund Road, turned west through North Suzhou Road, passed by the Postal Administration, and proceeded along North Sichuan Road and Pazilu. The original plan was to go to the North Station and proceed north along Baoshan Road to see the ruins of the Eastern Library and the Nanshi Library, which were destroyed in the war. Although the weather had cleared up, the visit was canceled due to time constraints. The motorcade then took Baoxing Road and Shuidian Road to the city center area and circled the City Hall. Mayor Wu stood in front of the City Hall and nodded and smiled to the athletes to show his welcome.

Visiting the Battle Sites: After leaving the City Hall, the motorcade entered Jungong Road, passed through Yunzaobing, and arrived at the Wusong Fort to visit the sites of the Songhu Battle. Soldiers there gave a detailed account of the battle and the destruction suffered. Once a military fortress for our national defense, today it is overgrown with weeds, a desolate scene. The overseas Chinese athletes were saddened by the sight and could not help but sigh. After leaving the fort, they returned to the City Hall to meet with Mayor Wu. In addition to offering words of encouragement to the athletes, he also hosted them in the auditorium, serving refreshments. By then, dusk had fallen, and they bid farewell and returned to the dormitories of the Liangjiang Women's School to rest.

Municipal Education Bureau Announcement Regarding School Transportation Arrangements for Spectators

The Shanghai Education Bureau issued an announcement yesterday regarding school transportation arrangements for spectators at the Sixth National Games, stating: "The Sixth National Games has commenced. During the Games, a large number of students will be attending as spectators, and it is imperative to plan for transportation to facilitate their attendance. After discussions between this bureau and the Public Utilities Bureau and the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, a special train will be dispatched daily from the South Railway Station at 11:30 AM, going directly to the Sanmin Road stadium in the city center. At 6:30 PM, the train will return from Sanmin Road to the South Station, stopping at Longhua, Xujiahui, and Fanwangdu stations. This special train will be limited to 1,500 passengers per day, with a round-trip fare of 50 cents per person. Schools located in the South and West districts of the city and near the stations should use this special train if they do not have their own transportation. Schools should provide an official letter and send a representative to the South Station Master to make reservations one day before their scheduled visit to avoid last-minute rush. Additionally, during the Games, the Zhabei Business Public Bus Company will add buses on the Baoxing Road-Shuidian Road route, and there will be approximately 200 large trucks with modified seating departing from Yunli Road behind Hongkou Park (south of the Sports Garden) directly to the stadium every day. Each truck can accommodate 50 people, with departures approximately every minute. Schools in and around Zhabei should be able to use these trucks. Furthermore, there are steam trains from the North Station on Songhu Road that go directly to the stadium, with a fare of 15 cents per person per trip. Those traveling from Wusong to the venue will need to change trains at Gaojingmiao. This announcement is hereby issued for general knowledge." Issued on October 8th, 1935 by Director Pan Gongzhan of the Bureau.

Games Referees Meeting Today at 3:00 PM at De Lin Apartments

All Games referees are scheduled to meet at 3:00 PM today at De Lin Apartments (separate arrangements for national martial arts referees). Badges, order books, special competition regulations, and various competition rules will be distributed at the same time. Due to limited seating at the apartments, line judges for tennis and volleyball are only requested to collect the above items for use during the Games, and attendance at the meeting is waived. The meeting will be divided into two groups: one for track and field, all-around, and swimming, and the other for ball games, each occupying one floor (as the same floor cannot accommodate so many people). In addition to reporting matters, Mr. Zhang Boling will be invited to give a speech on "The Responsibility of Referees." Subsequently, the head referees will lead small group discussions separately (e.g., head referees for various ball games, finish line referees, field referees, head timers, inspectors, chief recorders, etc.) in the hope of enhancing the effectiveness of service.

Sichuan Track and Field Team Loses to Chih Chih College

—83 to 46—

Qiu Zhongcheng Breaks National Record in 3,000 Meters; Sichuan Team's Talent is Average, Lacking Competitive Strength

To improve their skills, the Sichuan track and field team participating in the National Games specially arranged a friendly competition yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM with the Chih Chih College track and field team at the Chih Chih field. Chih Chih College boasts many Shanghai representatives participating in the National Games, including Dai Shuguo, Lin Shaozhou, Zhang Jialing, Qiu Zhongcheng, Hong Rongtang, Ma Qingyuan, and Li Houda. The Sichuan team's talent is average, so there was no fierce competition. Qiu Zhongcheng's performance in the 3,000 meters was the most outstanding, breaking the national record with a time of 9 minutes 56.6 seconds. Li Houda's performance in the intermediate hurdles was also strong, with a time of 1 minute, approaching the national record. In the end, Chih Chih College defeated Sichuan with a score of 83 to 46. The results are listed below:

The office also includes a branch of the Water Restaurant, offering exquisite Chinese and Western refreshments at reasonable prices. All patrons will receive a free copy of the National Games handbook published by the company.

Telegraph Bureau Establishes Temporary Office The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has established a temporary office at the National Games venue and has installed several of the latest telegraph machines to transmit various competition results at any time starting today. Athletes from all provinces participating in this National Games will receive special preferential rates for sending telegrams, which is especially convenient for them.

Sichuan Delegation Leader Returns to Shanghai After Paying Respects at Mausoleum Liu Shenzhan, the leader of the Sichuan delegation, was elected by all staff and athletes to represent them in paying respects at the mausoleum in Nanjing and visiting senior party and government officials. Mr. Liu took a train to Nanjing on the evening of the 6th and arrived on the 7th. He then accompanied several fellow provincials on a special trip to the mausoleum to pay respects to the tomb of Sun Yat-sen and offer a wreath. He hastily returned to Shanghai yesterday morning.

Shaanxi Students Association in Shanghai Tea Party The Shaanxi Students Association in Shanghai held a tea party yesterday afternoon at 6:00 PM on the second floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA to welcome the Shaanxi athletes participating in the National Games. Attendees included Zhang Zihui, Ai Zigao, and over a dozen others. Wang Kemin, Shi Shijie, and Li Jingxi of the association gave welcoming speeches and reports.

Macao Table Tennis Team to Play Shanghai Guangdong Team Tonight

Since table tennis has been included as a demonstration event in this National Games, elite table tennis players from all over have gathered in this city. The Macao table tennis team is particularly strong, with a wealth of talent, truly a powerful team from Southern China. As table tennis is particularly developed in Guangdong and this city, and the Macao team was able to win the championship and runner-up titles in the Guangdong Provincial Games table tennis competition this year, one can imagine their high level of skill. Since the team arrived in Shanghai, the Guangdong team, which has long enjoyed a reputation in this city, has arranged a friendly competition with the Macao team tonight at 8:00 PM at the Yokohama Bridge Central Auditorium to promote goodwill and improve skills. The names of the Macao team players are as follows: Zheng Guorong, Huang Shuinian, Liang Wenhuan, Guan Yongpu, Chen Guowei, Hu Jinying, Yang Jinchen, Lei Xueqin, and Feng Maosheng.

Fudan's 30th Anniversary Celebration: Second Day's Grand Occasion

Exhibition of Achievements Extremely Substantial, Football Match Brothers Very Courteous, Photography Achievements Excellent, Music Delightful

Fudan University in Jiangwan, celebrating its 30th anniversary, has a special three-day holiday for celebrations. The grand and solemn ceremony was held the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the exhibition rooms were still open as usual. After lunch, there were two major activities: a football match and a musical performance. The details are recorded below:

A Glimpse of Achievements: This time, each department has an exhibition of achievements, located in Jian Gong Hall, the newspaper exhibition, the photography exhibition room, the literature, law, and business departments, and the exhibition of industrial and national goods. The science department is in Zibin Hall. The library is purely for academic exhibition. Because the content is substantial and not falsified, the true face is displayed to the society. Viewers are constantly on the road, unanimously praising it. Especially noteworthy is the newspaper exhibition, which has a rich collection of world newspapers and multiple printing presses, operating on-site, with extremely accurate statistics.

Photography Exhibition: The photography association does not cater to social interests with nude photos, and all are automatically enlarged. One hundred and fifty works are displayed, a feast for the eyes, too beautiful to behold. It is said that it will be extended to the 10th to avoid viewers missing out.

Football Match: The football match was played in the rain. With a whistle from the referee, the brothers began to cross legs. The students of our school are young and strong, running very fast. The alumni are old but their knives are not dull, and they are exceptionally slippery. Everyone did not compete for victory or defeat, but went back and forth, very politely, until the sky was dark, then they sounded the gong to call it a day.

Musical Performance: The school's music group includes five teams, including a singing team, a string orchestra, and a harmonica team. The singing team has participated in off-campus performances several times, and the string orchestra has also performed once, both receiving social praise. The joint performance last night was truly rare. No wonder the gymnasium was packed. After the meeting, the sound of the zither and songs lingered, evoking the feeling of lingering sound for three days. It is said that there will be a Peking opera performance tomorrow night, and it is expected that the grand occasion will be no less than this.

Opening Ceremony of Denghui Hall at Fudan Affiliated High School

The Affiliated High School of Fudan University in this city, in commemoration of Dr. Li Denghui's thirty years of service to Fudan, held the opening ceremony of Denghui Hall during the celebration of the school's thirtieth anniversary. The number of participants included former school principal Ma Xiangbo, Ambassador to Germany Cheng Tianfang, Special Zone Court President Guo Yunguan, Zhejiang Provincial Government Secretary-General Huang Ermin, Education Bureau Representative Chen Bai, International Labor Bureau China Branch Director Cheng Haifeng, guests Zhu Shaoping, Su Er, Principal of McLaren Middle School Shen Tilan, Gu Tianfang of Nanyang Middle School, representatives of the Board of Directors Jiang Yiping and Zhu Zhonghua, representatives of the Alumni Association Xi Yushu, and the school's University Secretary-General Jin Tongyin, Business School Dean Li Quanshi, Law School Deans Zhang Zhirang, Zhang Youliang, Sun Hanyong, and Gu Zhongyi, old classmates Bi Jingqian, Zhu Yizhou, Song Xiquan, Wu Falai, alumni of the affiliated high school, and more than 600 people. At that moment, firecrackers and applause rang out. Then Ma Xiangbo gave a speech, explaining that the meaning of Denghui Hall is to ascend to the path of light. Principal Li, Director Chen, Jiang Yiping, Guo Yunguan, Huang Ermin, Xi Yushu, Shen Tilan, and Cheng Haifeng gave speeches successively. The ceremony was completed. The school principal and director accompanied the guests to visit the achievements of various departments, such as student handicrafts and charts. In the evening, there were fireworks and entertainment to add to the excitement.

Chapter 5: The Mischievous Little Girl

One day after class, Mrs. Pei saw Mr. Pei and said, "Frederick, I have a new idea."

"Oh, my dear, what is it?" he said, listening attentively to her new plan, because many of her ideas were so humorous and absurd that one couldn't help but laugh, but they were generally quite reasonable, so he was happy to implement them.

"Little Mei needs a companion. It would also be good for the boys to have another girl to accompany them. You know, we believe in cultivating little men and little women together. Now is the time for us to put our ideals into practice, and we can't delay any longer. They either treasure Little Mei too much or abuse her, and her temper has already deteriorated as a result. They should know how to be gentle and refined, how to treat people with courtesy. To achieve this, it is more effective to have girls around than anything else."

"You are really insightful. Which one should we recruit now?" Mr. Pei asked, knowing from his wife's expression that she had already prepared a candidate to propose. So she replied:

"Little Annie Howe."

"What! Is that the one the children nicknamed 'Naughty Nan'?" Mr. Pei asked in surprise, looking like he was about to laugh again.

Special Issue for the 15th Anniversary of Meiya Silk Weaving Factory

Eulogy

— Zhang Gongquan

Silk is an essential item for human life. In the past, it was made by hand, but now it is made by machine. The difference in speed and quantity is known to everyone. Since the opening of the sea, steamships have frequently arrived. There are many kinds of cloth, and the value is cheap. There are even more kinds of silk, and the value is even cheaper. In the past, the products of Wu and Yue were almost completely taken away, and the annual loss of profits overseas cannot be counted in tens of thousands. During this period, enlightened people quickly started to catch up, competing to purchase machinery and establish factories to try to save the situation. The gains and losses varied, and it was not necessarily guaranteed to win. However, Meiya Silk Weaving Factory is different. Its planning is meticulous, its equipment is complete, its products are of high quality, and its patterns are novel, all of which are unmatched by other factories. Moreover, it can persevere with perseverance. In the past ten years, it has expanded from small to large, and from separate to combined, with a vibrant and promising atmosphere, which is truly admirable. I hope that its products will be promoted from within the country to beyond the country, from Asia to Europe and America, so that everyone will praise and admire them, and praise our silk products as the best in the world. Isn't that wonderful? Now, with the special issue for the 15th anniversary, I am happy to write this preface to encourage them.
